class="typography_body-l__v5JLj typography_appearance-default__t8iAq" data-service-review-text-typography="true">I am only giving 1 star because I can’t give none. I have just visited Burger King at Euston and received terrible service. 2 of us wanted 9 chilli bites but they were about £5.66 each, whereas 20 were £7.66. We asked for 20, as we saw that they had just made a whole batch (conservative estimate 120 pieces). However, we were told that there was a 20 minute wait for 20 pieces. This is obviously a money making scam as when we offered to accept 18 for the price of 20, they refused to serve us on that basis. They then had the cheek to tell us that we had to pay 40p for mayonnaise. This is all very unsatisfactory in itself, but the rudeness of the staff when we asked for an explanation of the pricing policy was astonishing. Can I suggest an alternative vendor if you are in Euston!</p><p class="typography_body-m__k2UI7 typography_appearance-default__t8iAq" data-service-review-date-of-experience-typography="true"><b
